On the title:
MMW 'vṛṣa':  "Justice or Virtue personified as a bull or as "Siva's bull Mn. viii, 16 Pur. Kāvyād.; just or virtuous act, virtue, moral merit "Siś. Vās.;"

On the title, see De Simini 2016:238 n. 13: ''As noted by Sanderson [...], this title can have a double meaning, since the ‘bull’ (vṛṣa) is both a synonym of ‘religious practice’ and the traditional mount (vāhana) of Śiva.

'Muta cum liquida' (Balogh 2018?:33 note 6) find sources on metrical licenses / -ces
Apte Appendix A p. 1: pra, bra, hra, kra are exceptions
In the text below, śra, śya, śva, sva, dva seem additional ones (plus tra and vra? and rp? 11.5X)

''According to Kedārabhaṭṭa in Vṛttaratnākara, a short vowel followed by a consonant cluster (i.e., multiple consonants), although guru by default, can optionally be treated as laghu if that consonant cluster happens to be the beginning of a new word. Implement this option. (With required UI changes, e.g. saying: "this verse can be read as <...> if an option is used in places x, y, z.") ''
SOURCE: ( https://github.com/shreevatsa/sanskrit/issues/1 )

Vṛttaratnākara 1.10! (etext downloaded):
padādāv iha varṇasya saṃyogaḥ kramasaṃjñikaḥ /
puraḥsthitena tena syāl laghutā 'pi kvacid guroḥ // KVrk_1.10 //

SOURCE: ( https://github.com/shreevatsa/sanskrit/issues/1 ):
``The traditional rule is that the presence of a conjunct consonant (consonant cluster) makes the preceding syllable a guru syllable. For purists, this is an inviolable rule, and there are no exceptions.

However, under the influence of Prākṛta and deśa-bhāṣā prosody, and also music, later prosodists give poets the option to either conform to this rule, or to occasionally indulge in an exception. This exception is stated differently by different authors:

    In Kannada and Telugu prosody, under the name of śithila-dvitva, the exception is that sometimes in a consonant cluster of the form [consonant + "r"], the "r" (repha) can be ignored, so that it is not a conjunct consonant anymore.
    Kedāra-bhaṭṭa in his Vṛtta-ratnākara states the exception as: if the consonant cluster is at the beginning of a word, then it may be treated as a single consonant.
    Yet another way of stating the exception is that a consonant cluster can be optionally treated as a single consonant if the effort of pronouncing it is quick (तीव्रप्रयत्नेन) or with less effort (श्रममन्तरा).

All ways of stating the exception cover the example of "निद्रव्यो ह्रियमेति ह्रीपरिगतः प्रभ्रश्यते तेजसः", but Kedārabhaṭṭa's way doesn't cover the example of "राज्ञां मध्ये सपदि जह्रिषे मित्रविन्दामवन्तीम्" from the Nārāyaṇīyam. So far I don't see a reason to prefer Kedārabhaṭṭa's formulation over the others.

But anyway, to return to the main point:

    The exception is not accepted by purists: Shatavadhani Ganesh says that the Sanskrit masters like Kālidāsa, Bhāravi, Māgha, Śrīharṣa, and Viśākhadatta have not freely used this exception (though the masters in Kannada and other languages have).
    Being more of a "poetic licence" and a violation of the standard rule (only found in later poetry), it is extremely unlikely that any sane poet would have indulged in that exception in all four pāda-s of a verse.
    Thus it is very unlikely that the program will miss identifying a verse that indulges in this exception. At least, I haven't seen any example from real life so far. (Just saying that because it would be easy to intentionally compose a verse to disproves this!)

Reference: see comments by Dr. Ganesh and Nityananda Misra in this thread started by Vishvas Vasuki:
https://groups.google.com/forum/#!topic/bvparishat/ya1cGLuhc14/discussion
''

Nirajan's advice was to look into Chandomañjarī, and here you are:

atra pādāntago laghur gurur bhaved| yathā| 
taruṇaṃ va?rṣapaśākaṃ navaudanaṃ picchilāni ca dadhīni?|
alpavyayena sundari grāmyajano miṣṭam aśnāti||
sundarīti grāmyaśabde pare [because it is followed by the word grāmya] vikalpena [option] laghutvam|
tathā bhaṭṭiḥ|

lulitapatatrimālaṃ rugṇāśanavāṇakesaratamālam|

IDEAS:
- is this text really Śaiva? why in this collection?
- niśvāsa as sadāśiva in ch. 16; Niśvāsa uttarasūtra 5.50-51; see also Kafle Niśvāsamukha p.11ff; ibid. p.12: "The term niśvāsa means sighing. Thus, an alternative
meaning of the Niśvāsatattvasaṃhitā could also be a ‘‘sighing tantra.’’ To be more precise,
a tantra that originated from the sighing of Śiva. This is to say, the speech of Śiva."
- tattva-system: mati and suśira (ch. 20)
- parallels: MBh, Bṛhatkālottara, 
- ch. 21: Viṣṇu; is this a Śaiva text?
- āśramas are in an order different from usual; compare this to NĀT; "Variations on the āśrama-system"

History of Dharmasastra 2.1
pp. 416ff on āśramas

n. 988! see Āpastamba-dharma-sūtra ii.9.21.1: catvāra āśramā gārhasthyam ācāryakulaṃ maunaṃ vānaprasthyam iti| Quoted by Śankara
But the chapters in Āpastamba follow the traditional order.
"Āp. places the householder first among the āśramas, probably on account of the importance of that stage to all other āśramas." Kane ibid.

ibid p. 417: person in last āśrama is called: parivrāṭ, parivrājaka(!), bhikṣu, muni, yati.
See 
Olivelle, Patrick. The Āśrama System. The History and Hermeneutics of a Religious Institution. New York, Oxford: Oxford University Press, 1993.  [megvan] p.82ff: The Order of Āśramas; 
        ibid: "In later texts the usual order is student, householder, hermit, and renouncer, reflecting the sequence of the passage from one _āśrama_ to another... In the Dharmasūtras, however, only Baudhāyana and Vasiṣṭha follow that order... A specific order becomes insignificant when the _āśramas_ are taken as four alternative adult vocations." 
Are they alternative adult vocations here in the Vṛṣasārasaṃgraha? They are numbered.

\textit{Gṛhastha. The Householder in Ancient Indian 
Religious Culture.} Edited by Patrick Olivelle. OUP, 2019.
Especially Csaba Dezső's article in it.

% CHECK if Naraharinath seems to be better at Sanskrit in other texts
% the edition seems problematic at many places
% a dialogue between Janamejaya and Vaiśampāyana, the latter of whom relates
dialogues between Vigatarāga and Anarthayajña
% revise *s and lost/ill
Bisschop in "Universal Śaivism": " – En-dashes indicate a lost or illegible syllable in the manuscript."

%N. of a celebrated king to whom Vaiśampāyana recited the [MBh.] (greatgrandson to Arjuna, as being son and, successor to Parikshit who was the son of Arjuna's son Abhimanyu) ["SBr.] xi, xīi AitBr. "Sāṅkhir. xvi [MBh.] &c.;

Bisschop 2018:2:
``The full text of the corpus was first published by Naraharinātha in 1998, while over the past few years several scholars have started to work on individual parts of the corpus or referred to them in their studies. See, in particular, Acharya 2009; Bisschop 2010, 2014; De Simini 2013, 2016a, 2016b, 2017; De Simini & Mirnig 2017; Goodall 2011; Kafle 2013, 2015; Magnone 2005; Sanderson 2003/04, 2012/13; Schwartz 2012. An edition of the Śivadharmaśāstra alone, based on a single manuscript in the Adyar Library, has been published more recently as well (Jugnu & Sharma 2014). The Śivopaniṣad, which also forms part of the Śivadharma corpus, was already published much earlier but was not recognised as such, being included in a collection of Upaniṣads (Kunhan Raja 1933).''

What MS did Naraharinātha used? See Biscchop 2018:58--59.

24 chapters?

smārta, bhārata)

On birth:

Vipula in the MBh:

	MBh 13040016aff

	Devaśarman and his wife Ruci
	13040017a tasya rūpeṇa --> 13040017a tasyā rūpeṇa

	all gods, esp. Indra, are in love with her
	but Devaśarman guards her
	wants to perform yajña: how to guard her during the ritual?
	calls his pupil, Vipula
	tells him that Indra can assume various forms
	Vipula decides that the only way to protect her from Indra is to magically 'enter' her (with yoga)
	he tells her stories and enters her 

	MBh 13041001ff
	Indra sees the opportunity and enters the āśrama as a beautiful man
	he sees Vipula's lifeless body
	Ruci fancies Indra, but Vipula in his body stops her from standing up
	Indra sings to her beautiful songs
	he says "I have come for you, I am Devendra, I am in love"
	Vipula stops her from doing anything
	Indra is a bit shocked by her not being moved, gets angry and can see now that Vipula is in her
	Vipula leaves her, enters his own body, and abuses Indra and tells Indra how wicked he is
	Indra is ashamed and disappears
	Devaśarman returns to the āśrama, Vipula tells him what happened and Devaśarman praises him

        ETC., see translation here:
        https://www.sacred-texts.com/hin/m13/m13b005.htm

        See summary also here:
        V. S. Sukthankar. Critical Studies in the Mahābhārata.
                Poona, V. S. Sukthankar Memorial Edition Committee, 1944. 317--318
        https://archive.org/details/in.ernet.dli.2015.281344/page/n333

<TEXT> sukṛtaṃ duṣkṛtaṃ caiva pāśadvayam{ }udāhṛtam||</TEXT>
        <!-- <TR>Good and bad deeds are called the two nooses.</TR> -->

<PARAL>Ł\vo cf.\ \MBh\ 1.77.16: $ na narmayuktaṃ vacanaṃ hinasti na strīṣu rājan{ }na vivāhakāle|
        prāṇātyaye sarvadhanāpahāre pañcānṛtāny{ }āhur{ }apātakāni||;

<TEXT> snānaṃ divyaṃ vadaty{ }eva jagadādimaheśvaraḥ||</TEXT>

<TEXT> vigatarāga uvāca|*</TEXT>
<TEXT> katamaṃ sarvatīrthānāṃ śreṣṭham{ }āhur{ }manīṣinaḥ|</TEXT>

        <APP>\vb <LEM>manīṣinaḥ</LEM> \msCa; manīṣibhiḥ \Ed</APP>

        <APP>\vd <LEM>bhuvi</LEM> \msCa; bhūri \Ed</APP>
<TEXT> anarthayajña uvāca|*</TEXT>

<TEXT> ! saṃsāroddharaṇam{ }anityaharaṇam{ }ajñānanirmūlanam </TEXT>
        <!-- <TR>[If the yogin] follows, with faith and self-control, the supreme Dharma,
             which delivers him from Saṃsāra, removes transient existence, uproots ignorance,</TR> -->
        <APP>\va <LEM>°haraṇam{ }anityaharaṇam{ }ajñā°</LEM> \msCa\msCb\msNaacorr\msNb\msNc; 
                                °haraṇaṃ anityaharaṇan{ }tajñā° \msNapcorr, 
                                °haraṇaṃm{ }anityaharaṇam{ }ajñā° \msCc\Ed</APP>
        <NOTE>\msNa\ only corrects °haraṇamanitya° to °haraṇam anitya°, 
               but its scribe probably meant an anusvāra at the end of °haraṇaṃ, 
               perhaps trying to correct the metre. He tries to correct the metre
               also with anityaharaṇan tajñā°.</NOTE>

        <!-- <TR>increases wisdom, yields fruit, delivers him from the flood of affliction,</TR> -->
        <APP>\vb \om\ \msNb</APP>
<APP>
                 <LEM>°karam{ }amogha°</LEM> \msCamsCbmsCc\msNa\ \unmetr; \om\ \msNb, °kam{ }amogha° \msNc,

<TEXT> parivrājakadharmo 'yaṃ kīrtayiṣyāmi tac{ }chṛṇu|</TEXT>
        <!-- <TR>Here follows the Parivrājaka's Dharma. Listen, I shall teach you about it.</TR> -->
        <APP>\vb <LEM>kīrtayiṣyāmi</LEM> \msCb\msCc\msNa\msNb\msNc\Ed; kīrtayi×mi \msCa</APP>

<TEXT> sukhaduḥkhaṃ samaṃ kṛtvā lobhamohavivarjitaḥ||</TEXT> 11.44
        <!-- <TR>Making joy and pain equal, he gets rid of greed and folly.</TR> -->
        <APP>\vc <LEM>°duḥkhaṃ</LEM> \msCb; °duḥkha \msCa\msCc\msNa\msNb\msNc\Ed</APP>

<APP>
                 <LEM>°varjitaḥ</LEM> \msCamsCbmsCc\msNa\msNc\Ed; °varjitāḥ \msNb</APP>
        <PARAL>\vd Ł cf.\ 4.71: $  
                     kāmaḥ krodhaś{ }ca lobhaś{ }ca mohaś{ }caiva caturvidhaḥ|
                     catuḥśatrur{ }nihantavyaḥ sarvathā vītakalmaṣaḥ||</PARAL>

<TEXT> varjayen{ }madhu māṃsāni paradārāṃś{ }ca varjayet|</TEXT>

<TEXT> brahmaṇo hṛdayaṃ viṣṇur{ }viṣṇoś{ }ca hṛdayaṃ śivaḥ|</TEXT>
        <!-- <TR>Brahmā's heart is Viṣṇu. Viṣṇu's heart is Śiva.</TR> -->
        <APP>\va <LEM>hṛdayaṃ</LEM>  \msCb\msCc\msNa\msNb\Ed; ×dayaṃ \msCa, hṛdaye \msNc</APP>
        <APP>\vab <LEM>viṣṇur{ }vi°</LEM> \msCa\msNa\Ed; viṣṇum{ }vi° \msCb, viṣṇu vi° \msCc\msNb\msNc</APP>

<TEXT> śivasya hṛdayaṃ saṃdhyā tasmāt{ }saṃdhyām{ }upāsayet||</TEXT> 11.59
        <!-- <TR>Śiva's heart is the Junctures of the day. Therefore he should worship the Junctures.</TR> -->
        <APP>\vd <LEM>°sayet</LEM> \msCa\msCc\msNb; °śayet \msCb\msNa, °śrayet \msNc\Ed</APP>
        <PARAL>\vo \kb\ Ł Saubhāgyabhāskara of Bhāskararāya ad Lalitāsahasranāmastotra 302: $
                brahmaṇo hṛdayaṃ viṣṇur{ }viṣṇor{ }api śivaḥ smṛtaḥ|
                śivasya hṛdayaṃ sandhyā tenopāsyā dvijātibhiḥ||
                iti kaśyapādivacanaiḥ kaurmapādmaskāndādinikhilapurāṇeṣu ca tatra 
                tatra devīkālikābrahmāṇḍamārkaṇḍeyādipurāṇeṣu bahuśaḥ 
                śaktirahasyadevībhāgavatatṛtīyaskandhādiṣu| </PARAL>

<TEXT> dhyāyen{ }nityam{ }atandrito hy{ }anupamaṃ vyaktātmavedyaṃ śivam|</TEXT>
        <!-- <TR>[the yogin] should always, unweariedly, meditate on matchless Śiva, 
             who is to be recognized as the manifested soul.</TR> -->
        <APP>\vb <LEM>°tandrito</LEM> \msCa\msNa\msNc\Ed; °nandrito \msCb, °tandriya \msCc, °tandriyaṃ \msNb</APP>

        <!-- <TR>By this merit, he reached heaven unobstructed.</TR> -->

        <APP>\vc <LEM>kula°</LEM> \msCb; kala° \msCa\Ed\
             \vd <LEM>bhārya eva</LEM> \msCa\Ed; bhāryam{ }eva \msCb</APP>
        <!-- <TR>I am a wife, who is for the protectors of the race, and a wife because I nourish.</TR> -->

<CHAPTER>13 garbhotpattiḥ</CHAPTER> 
<TEXT> devy{ }uvāca|*</TEXT>
<TEXT> ahiṃsātithyakānāṃ ca śruto dharmaḥ suvistaraḥ|</TEXT>
<TEXT> kiṃ na kurvanti manujāḥ sukhopāyaṃ mahat{ }phalam||</TEXT>
<TEXT> svaśarīrasthito yajñaḥ svaśarīre sthitaṃ tapaḥ|</TEXT>
<TEXT> svaśarīre sthitaṃ tīrthaṃ śruto vistarato mayā||</TEXT>
<TEXT> kimarthaṃ bhagavan{ }brūhi sukhopāyaṃ mahat{ }phalam|</TEXT>
<TEXT> kiṃ nivṛttās{ }tu deveśa ṛṣidaivatamānuṣāḥ||</TEXT>
<TEXT> mahādeva uvāca|*</TEXT>
        <APP>\vo <LEM>mahādeva</LEM> \msCa; bhagavān \Ed</APP>
<TEXT> adya pṛṣṭena kathitaṃ gopitaṃ ṛṣi sundari|</TEXT>
<TEXT> mānuṣāṇāṃ hitārthāya tava ca varavarṇini||</TEXT>
<TEXT> adyaprabhṛti deveśi khyātir{ }loke bhaviṣyati|</TEXT>
<TEXT> dhanyā evaṃ cariṣyanti adhanyā na ramanti tam||</TEXT>
<TEXT> triguṇena tu bandhena baddhā pāśadṛḍhena tu|</TEXT>
<TEXT> tenārthena ramanty{ }atra jānanto 'pi vimohitāḥ||</TEXT>
<TEXT> devy{ }uvāca|*</TEXT>
% cchedaka would be unmetrical?
<TEXT> kiṃ vā triguṇabandheti brūhi saṃśayachedaka|</TEXT>
<TEXT> adyāpi mama deveśa mohotpannas{ }tribandhanaiḥ||</TEXT>
<TEXT> bhagavān{ }uvāca|*</TEXT>
<TEXT> prākṛtaṃ vaikṛtaṃ caiva dakṣiṇābandham{ }eva ca|</TEXT>
<TEXT> etenaiva tu bandhena baddhāḥ varṇāśramāḥ sadā||</TEXT>
<TEXT> jñānahīnā nivartante paramaṃ prāpya tatparam|</TEXT>
<TEXT> iṣṭastrīṇā nivartante dhanadhānyasamuccaye|</TEXT>
<TEXT> snehād{ }ākṛṣya manasāṃ bandhaḥ prākṛta ucyate||</TEXT>
<TEXT> yogayuktena manasā yad{ }yad{ }aiśvaryam{ }āpyate|</TEXT>
<TEXT> tac{ }ca vaikṛtabandhas{ }tu yadi tatrānurajyate||</TEXT>
%Naraharinatha p.630
<TEXT> ārāmodyānavāpīṣu dānakratuphaleṣu ca|</TEXT>
%                        should be bandha metri causa
<TEXT> āśaktamanasā vācā dakṣiṇābandhaḥ kathyate||</TEXT>
<TEXT> anenaiva tu pāśena baddhāvānaravad{ }yathā|</TEXT>
<TEXT> mokṣitaṃ na ca śaknoti itaś{ }cetaś{ }ca dhāvati||</TEXT>
<TEXT> devāsuramanuṣyeṣu tiryeṣu narakeṣu ca|</TEXT>
<TEXT> bhramante cakrayantreva ? yāvat{ }tattvaṃ na vindati||</TEXT>
<TEXT> garbhavāsaparikleśau janmamṛtyu punaḥ punaḥ|</TEXT>
<TEXT> vyādhiḥ śokabhayāyāsa cintayā jarayā hataḥ||</TEXT>
<TEXT> devy{ }uvāca|*</TEXT>
<TEXT> garbhotpattiḥ kathaṃ deva yogī labhati kīdṛśīm|</TEXT>
<TEXT> kīdṛśaṃ labhate garbhaḥ śrotuṃ naḥ pratyudīryatām||</TEXT>
<TEXT> bhagavān{ }uvāca|*</TEXT>
<TEXT> śṛṇu devi pravakṣyāmi garbhotpattir{ }yathākramam|</TEXT>
<TEXT> yathā saṃśayavicchedaṃ bhaviṣyasi varānane||</TEXT>
<TEXT> akṣarāt{ }prabhavo brahmā karmabaddhasamudbhavam|</TEXT>
<TEXT> karmato yajñaprabhavo yajñato dhūmasambhavaḥ||</TEXT>
        <!-- <TR>From ritual arises sacrifice. From sacrifice arises smoke.</TR> -->
<TEXT> parjanyād{ }annam{ }utpattir{ }annād{ }bhūtāni jajñire|</TEXT>
        <!-- <TR>From the clouds food arises. From food living beings arise.</TR> -->
<TEXT> annād{ }rasasamutpatti rasāc{ }choṇitasambhavaḥ||</TEXT>
        <!-- <TR>From food arises rasa. From rasa arises blood.</TR> -->
<TEXT> śoṇitāt - māṃsa-m-utpatti māṃsād{ }medasamudbhavaḥ|</TEXT>
        <!-- <TR>From blood flesh arises. From flesh fat arises.</TR> -->
<TEXT> medaso 'sthīni jāyante asthibhyo majjasambhavaḥ||</TEXT>
        <!-- <TR>From fat bones arise. From the bones marrow arises.</TR> -->
<TEXT> majjāyās{ }tu bhavec{ }chukraṃ naraḥ śukrasamudbhavaḥ|</TEXT>
        <!-- <TR>From marrow arises semen. And man is born from semen.</TR> -->
<TEXT> śukraśoṇitasaṃyogād{ }garbhotpattis{ }tataḥ smṛtaḥ||</TEXT>
<TEXT> agnisomātmakaṃ devi śarīradvayadhātutaḥ|</TEXT>
<TEXT> somadhātusmṛtaṃ śukram{ }agnidhāturajasmṛtam|</TEXT>
<TEXT> agnisomāśrayaṃ devi śarīram{ }iti saṃjñitam||</TEXT>
<TEXT> māsī māsī ṛtuḥ strīṇāṃ bhavatīha na saṃśayaḥ|</TEXT>
<TEXT> ṛtukāle prasarpyeta na sukhārthaṃ varānane||</TEXT>
<TEXT> putrakāmaprayuñjīta dharmārthaś{ }ca yaśasvini|</TEXT>
<TEXT> pumān{ }strīpuṃ prayuñjīta araṇī bahutāśanaḥ||</TEXT>
<TEXT> pumān{ }śukrādhiko jñeyaḥ kanyā raktādhikā bhavet|</TEXT>
<TEXT> samaśukre ca rakte ca sa ca jāyen{ }napuṃsakaḥ||</TEXT>
%Naraharinatha p.631

<SUBCHAPTER>dviyamā triyamā ca gurviṇī</SUBCHAPTER>
<TEXT> devy{ }uvāca|*</TEXT>
<TEXT> dviyamā triyamā caiva kathaṃ jāyeta gurviṇī|</TEXT>
<TEXT> kathaṃ strīdviyamā jāyet{ }kathaṃ vā puruṣadvayam||</TEXT>
<TEXT> bhagavān{ }uvāca|*</TEXT>
<TEXT> raktādhikā smṛtā kanyā jāyate varavarṇini|</TEXT>
<TEXT> vāyunā ca dvidhā bhinnā kanyakadviyamā smṛtā||</TEXT>
<TEXT> śukrādhikās{ }tu puruṣa dvidhā bhinnānilena tu|</TEXT>
<TEXT> dviyamā puruṣo jñeyā triyamās{ }tu tridhā kṛte||</TEXT>
<TEXT> ṛtusnātā yadā nārī yadi garbhādi gṛhyati|</TEXT>
<TEXT> prathame ca dvitīye ca tṛtīye ca sa jīvati||</TEXT>
<TEXT> sameṣu janayet{ }putraḥ kanyakā viṣame dine|</TEXT>
<TEXT> ṣaṣṭyāṣṭamau ca daśamī dvādaśī ca pumān{ }bhavet||</TEXT>
<TEXT> pañcamī saptamī caiva navamekādaśī striyaḥ|</TEXT>
<TEXT> samarakte ca śukre ca śyāmaḥ saṃjāyate pumān||</TEXT>
<TEXT> rudhiraṃ tv{ }ekarātreṇa kalalaṃ pratipadyate|</TEXT>
<TEXT> kalalaṃ pañcarātreṇa arbudatvaṃ prajāyate||</TEXT>
<TEXT> arbudaḥ saptarātreṇa māṃsapeśī samudbhavaḥ|</TEXT>
% \kb\ Śivadharmottara 29ab
<TEXT> dvitīyaṃ saptarātreṇa tat{ }sarvaṃ māṃsaśoṇitam||</TEXT>
<TEXT> tṛtīyaṃ saptarātreṇa hṛdayaṃ jāyate tataḥ|</TEXT>
<TEXT> tataḥ sarvāṇi gātrāṇi śiraś{ }caivopajāyate||</TEXT>
<TEXT> hṛdaye jāyamāne tu mūrcchāntandrirarocakaḥ|</TEXT>
<TEXT> striyāḥ dhardiḥ praśekaś{ }ca daurbalyaṃ copajāyate||</TEXT>
<TEXT> tasyā hi hṛdayaṃ nārī yadi bhakṣyati kiṃcana|</TEXT>
% MSS bhidyati 
<TEXT> bhakṣyaṃ lohyaṃ tathā peyam{ }upabhogās{ }tathāyayat||</TEXT>
% lehyaṃ
<TEXT> śayanāśanayānāni vastrāṇy{ }ābharaṇāni ca|</TEXT>
<TEXT> yad{ }yad{ }ākāṃkṣate kiṃcit{ }tat{ }tad{ }āsyai pradāpayet||</TEXT>
        <PARAL> \vo ŁCf.\ MBh 13.40.12:$
        śayyāsanam alaṃkāram annapānam anāryatām
        durvāgbhāvaṃ ratiṃ caiva dadau strībhyaḥ prajāpatiḥ</PARAL>

<TEXT> nāyā saṃkārayec{ }cāsyā na caivam{ }avamānayet|</TEXT>
<TEXT> mukham{ }āpāṇḍuraṃ snigdhaṃ kapolastanakeśayoḥ||</TEXT>
<TEXT> śarīraś{ }ca śriyā jaṣṭuṃ pīnoruśroṇi vakṣasam|</TEXT>
<TEXT> liṅgerebhir{ }vijānīyāṃ garbhe jīvaṃ pratiṣṭhitam||</TEXT>
<TEXT> caturthe saptarātreṇa śiraś{ }caivopajāyate|</TEXT>
% unmetr (two short)
<TEXT> pañcamasaptarātreṇa grīvā tatropajāyate||</TEXT>
% unmetr (two short)
<TEXT> ṣaṣṭhamasaptarātreṇa skandhagātraṃ prajāyate|</TEXT>
%Naraharinatha p.632
<TEXT> saptamasaptarātreṇa pṛṣṭhavaṃśa prajāyate||</TEXT>
<TEXT> aṣṭamasaptarātreṇa pāṇī jāyate cobhayau|</TEXT>
<TEXT> saptarātraṃ nava prāpya jāyate hṛdi pañjaram||</TEXT>
<TEXT> daśame saptarātre ca pādau jāyate cobhau|</TEXT>
<TEXT> udaraś{ }copajāyeta saptaikādaśarātrike||</TEXT>
% unmetr (two short)
<TEXT> dvādaśasaptarātreṇa kukṣipārśveḥ prajāyate|</TEXT>
<TEXT> saptatraidaśarātreṇa kuṭisutropajāyate||</TEXT>
<TEXT> navaty{ }aṣṭamarāteṇa jāyate sūtraviṃśati|</TEXT>
<TEXT> saptapañcadaśāhena sarvamedaḥ prajāyate||</TEXT>
<TEXT> ṣoḍaśasaptarātreṇa athisarvāṇi jāyate|</TEXT>
<TEXT> saptasaptadaśāhena jāyate snāyubandhanam||</TEXT>
<TEXT> saptamāṣṭādaśāhena jāyate mukhamaṇḍalam|</TEXT>

<TEXT> saptaviṃśatirātreṇa naitranāliṃ prajāyate|</TEXT>
<TEXT> saptaikaviṃśarātreṇa karṇayugmaṃ prajāyate||</TEXT>

<TEXT> pañcaviṃśatisaptāhe jihvā jāyate sundari||</TEXT>

<TEXT> unaviṃśatisaptāhe jāyate ca tvag{ }eva ca||</TEXT>
% unmetr (two short)
<TEXT> triṃśatasaptarātreṇa jāyate nābhimaṇḍalam|</TEXT>
<TEXT> saptaikatriṃśarātreṇa sarvarandhraṃ prajāyate||</TEXT>
<TEXT> dvātriṃśasaptarātreṇa nakhaviṃśati jāyate|</TEXT>
<TEXT> tritriṃśasaptarātreṇa sarve sandhiḥ prajāyate||</TEXT>
<TEXT> pañcatriṃśati saptāhe sarvamarma prajāyate|</TEXT>
<TEXT> ṣaḍtriṃśasaptarātreṇa vedanā copajāyate||</TEXT>
<TEXT> saptatriṃśatisaptāhe īrṣyādveṣaḥ prajāyate|</TEXT>
<TEXT> aṣṭatriṃśatisaptāhe pañcātmakasamanvitam||</TEXT>
<TEXT> sarvāṅgam{ }aṅgasampūrṇaḥ paripakva(ḥ) sa tiṣṭhati|</TEXT>
<TEXT> mātusvāśitapītaś{ }ca nābhisūtrāganena tu||</TEXT>
%Naraharinatha p.633
<TEXT> ajātasyopadhāryante garbhasthasyaiva jantavaḥ|</TEXT>
<TEXT> tataḥ praviśate dehe nidrāsvapna yathā tathā||</TEXT>
<TEXT> nopalabhyati sūkṣmatvād{ }araṇy{ }agnir{ }yathā tathā|</TEXT>
<TEXT> garbhodakena siktāṅgajarāyā pariveṣṭitaḥ||</TEXT>
<TEXT> jāti smarati tatrastho jantuś{ }cetaḥsamanvitaḥ|</TEXT>
<TEXT> mṛtaś{ }cāhaṃ punarjāto bhūyaś{ }caiva punarmṛtaḥ||</TEXT>
% \kb\ Śivadharmottara 39ab 
<TEXT> sthāvarāṇāṃ sahasreṣu jāto 'smi vividheṣu ca|</TEXT>
<TEXT> caturvarṇavivarṇeṣu mānuṣeṣu sahasraśaḥ||</TEXT>
<TEXT> sāmprataṃ ca punar{ }garbhaḥ kleśaḥ prāptaḥ suduḥsahaḥ|</TEXT>
<TEXT> idānīṃ jātamātro 'haṃ saṃskāraiś{ }cāpi saṃskṛtaḥ||</TEXT>
% similar to Śivadharmottara 40ab
<TEXT> yogam{ }evābhisevāmi sā[ṃ]khyaṃ vā pañcaviṃśakam|</TEXT>
<TEXT> yatra janmajarā nāsti yatra mṛtyuś{ }ca nāsti vai||</TEXT>
<TEXT> yatra brahma paraṃ vedyaṃ cariṣyāmi yatavrataḥ|</TEXT>
<TEXT> evam{ }ādīny{ }anekāni cintayitvā punaḥ punaḥ||</TEXT>
<TEXT> yāvat{ }tiṣṭhati garbhastho jāti smarati pūrvikām|</TEXT>
<TEXT> tato jāyati kaṣṭena mahākleśena mānavaḥ||</TEXT>
<TEXT> yoniyantrasutīvreṇa pīḍyamānasuduḥkhitaḥ|</TEXT>
<TEXT> jātamātrosmṛtibhraṃśo bhavatīha acetaneḥ||</TEXT>
<TEXT> māyāmudgaratīvreṇa hataḥ kiṃ śubham{ }ācaret|</TEXT>
<TEXT> eṣa garbhasamutpattiḥ kathito 'smi varānane|</TEXT>
<TEXT> duḥkhasaṃsārapraśamaṃ kiṃ bhūyaḥ śrotum{ }icchasi||</TEXT>
<TEXT> <COLOPHON>iti vṛṣasārasaṃgrahe garbhotpattir{ }nāma trayadaśo ! 'dhyāyaḥ</COLOPHON></TEXT>

<TEXT> atidīrghātihrasvaś{ }ca pumān{ }kenopajāyate|</TEXT>

<TEXT> bhagavān{ }uvāca|*</TEXT>
<TEXT> gṛhītagarbhā yā nārī nityam{ }uttānaśālinī|</TEXT>
<TEXT> prasāritavimuktātmā so 'tidīrghaḥ prajāyate||</TEXT>
%Naraharinatha p.634
<TEXT> gṛhītagarbhā yā nārī śete saṃkucitā sadā|</TEXT>
<TEXT> raso 'nnādīni kaṭukaṃ sevanāḥ hrasva jāyate||</TEXT>
<TEXT> gṛhītagarbhā yā nārī nityaṃ kṣīropasevitā|</TEXT>
<TEXT> varakodravaśālī ca bhuktā cāpi yavodanam||</TEXT>
% sāti- ! for sa ati double sandhi
<TEXT> śuklavastrasrajā yuktā sātigauraṃ prajāyate|</TEXT>
<TEXT> gṛhītagarbhā yā nārī bāladhānyāni sevate||</TEXT>

<TEXT> kṛṣṇavastrasrajādīni tasyāḥ kṛṣṇaḥ prajāyate||</TEXT>
<TEXT> devy{ }uvāca|*</TEXT>
<TEXT> jātyandho jāyate kasmānṣaṇḍhobhīrur{ }hatendriyaḥ|</TEXT>
<TEXT> kujo vā vāmano vāpi paṅgavaḥ sthūlaśiraḥ katham||</TEXT>
<TEXT> bhagavān{ }uvāca|*</TEXT>
<TEXT> gṛhītagarbhā yā nārī tīkṣṇoṣṇāny{ }upasevate|</TEXT>
<TEXT> laśunānipalāṇḍūni karañjamūlakāni ca||</TEXT>
<TEXT> pippalīśṛṅgaveraṃ ca sarṣapānmaricāni ca|</TEXT>
<TEXT> āsavaś{ }ca parikliṣṭā ye cānye kaṭutiktakāḥ||</TEXT>
<TEXT> tīkṣṇaṃ tu sevamānā yā jātyandho jāyate sutaḥ|</TEXT>
<TEXT> mithyāpacārāḥ strīpuṃso vyāpanne śukraśoṇite|</TEXT>
<TEXT> yadā garbhāśaye raktaṃ striyāḥ pūrvaṃ niṣicyate||</TEXT>
<TEXT> paścāc{ }chukraṃ raktakāle tadāṣaṇḍaḥ prajāyate|</TEXT>
<TEXT> trastodvigno yadā bhītastrīpuṃsāṃsūpajāyate||</TEXT>
<TEXT> tatra yo jāyate garbhabhiruḥ krandanako bhavet|</TEXT>
<TEXT> nisargakāle śukrasya vighna utpadyate yadā||</TEXT>
<TEXT> indriyāvartavighne tu tadā jāyed{ }atindriyaḥ| </TEXT>
<TEXT> gṛhītagarbhā yā nārī vātalāny{ }upasevate||</TEXT>
<TEXT> kaṭukāni kaṣāyāni tiktāni ca viśeṣataḥ|</TEXT>
<TEXT> vātaḥ prakupitas{ }tasyā garbham ātuhya tiṣṭhati||</TEXT>
<TEXT> kubjas{ }tu jāyate tasmād{ }garbhād{ }vātanipīḍanāt|</TEXT>
<TEXT> nityasāsavaśīlāyā tathā cotkaṭukāśanā||</TEXT>
<TEXT> tasyā saṃhanyate garbho vāmanas{ }tena jāyate|</TEXT>
<TEXT> ativyāyāmaśīlā tu ya nārī viṣamāsanī||</TEXT>
<TEXT> garbhaḥ saṃkṣubhyate tasyāḥ paṣaṇḍas{ }tenopajāyate|</TEXT>
%Naraharinatha p.635
<TEXT> </TEXT>

<TEXT> gṛhītagarbhā yā nārī rūkṣadhānyāni sevate||</TEXT>
<TEXT> vātaśleṣmaśirastho vai tasyā garbhasya kupyate|</TEXT>
<TEXT> tataḥ sthūlaśirās{ }tena pumān{ }jāyaty{ }asaṃśayaḥ||</TEXT>
<TEXT> devy{ }uvāca|*</TEXT>
<TEXT> karālāṅgā hanuḥ paṅgūr{ }mūko gadgadabhāṣakaḥ|</TEXT>
<TEXT> vikṛtākṣas{ }tv{ }anakṣo vā bhavadrasvagudaḥ katham||</TEXT>
<TEXT> bhagavān{ }uvāca|*</TEXT>
<TEXT> karālas{ }tena doṣeṇa jāyate mānavas{ }tathā|</TEXT>
% vipula

<TEXT> gṛhītagarbhā yā nārī madhurāṇy{ }upasevate||</TEXT>
%Naraharinatha p.636
<TEXT> śṛṅgāṭakakalotyāni śālūkāni viśāni ca|</TEXT>
<TEXT> mocaṃ tālaphalaṃ caiva nārikelaphalaṃ tathā||</TEXT>
<TEXT> atikṣṇaṃ sevamānā tu adhikāṅgaṃprasūyate|</TEXT>
<TEXT> piṅgākṣaḥ śleṣmapittābhyāṃ śvetākṣaḥ śleṣmaṇā bhavet||</TEXT>
<TEXT> devy{ }uvāca|*</TEXT>
<TEXT> kathaṃ vā jāyate putraḥ kanyakā kena jāyate|</TEXT>
<TEXT> apumān{ }kena jāyeta dviyamā triyamā tathā||</TEXT>
<TEXT> bhagavān{ }uvāca|*</TEXT>
<TEXT> śukrādhikaḥ pumān{ }jñeyaḥ kanyā raktādhikā bhavet|</TEXT>
<TEXT> raktaśukrasamatvena jāyate sa napuṃsakaḥ||</TEXT>
<TEXT> piṇdībhūto yadā garbha mārutau vibhaved{ }dvidhā|</TEXT>
<TEXT> evaṃ te dviyamā jñeyās{ }triyamā ca tridhā kṛte||</TEXT>
<TEXT> devy{ }uvāca|*</TEXT>
<TEXT> śoṇitaṃ māṃsa medaś{ }ca asthi majjā ca pañcamī|</TEXT>
<TEXT> śarīrasthāni dṛśyante śukrasthānaṃ na dṛśyate||</TEXT>
<TEXT> tasyotpattiś{ }ca sthānaṃ ca jñātum{ }icchāmi tattvataḥ|</TEXT>
%                                                  -am
<TEXT> kathayasva trilokeśa cchettum{ }arhasi saṃśayaḥ||</TEXT>
<TEXT> bhagavān{ }uvāca|*</TEXT>
<TEXT> manaḥ śukrasya prabhavaṃ ghrāṇaṃ śrotraṃ tathākṣiṇī|</TEXT>
<TEXT> sthānaṃ tu sarvāṅgasamasparśāt{ }sparśaḥ pravartate||</TEXT>
<TEXT> yathā niṣiktaṃ kṣīraṃ tu payasād{ }dadhi jāyate|</TEXT>
<TEXT> pramathyamānadadhnas{ }tu sarpiso 'pi tathāgamaḥ||</TEXT>
% stem form? śarīra
<TEXT> evaṃ śarīra nirgaccet - śukraṃ śukravahā śirāḥ|</TEXT>
<TEXT> pūrayitvānupūrveṇa asthayo pratipadyate||</TEXT>
% end is unmetr
<TEXT> tatas{ }tu tāḥ śukravahā meḍhranābhīm{ }anusṛtāḥ|</TEXT>
<TEXT> nāśukraṃ tat{ }tu siñcanti tasmād{ }garbhasya sambhavaḥ||</TEXT>
%Naraharinatha p.637
<TEXT> devy{ }uvāca|*</TEXT>
<TEXT> kathaṃ vedayate jāti kathaṃ jātismaro bhavet|</TEXT>
% note the vocative to Śiva
<TEXT> etasmin{ }saṃśayaṃ me 'dya chettum{ }arhasi śaṅkara||</TEXT>
<TEXT> bhagavān{ }uvāca|*</TEXT>
<TEXT> bhāvitātmāṃ ca yo jantur{ }devi bhogādhikaṃ ca yat|</TEXT>
<TEXT> brahmavid{ }jñānasaṃyuktaḥ sa jātiṃ smarate pumān||</TEXT>
<TEXT> devy{ }uvāca|*</TEXT>
<TEXT> kathaṃ sadyo gṛhītasya liṅgagarbhasya dṛśyate|</TEXT>
<TEXT> etat{ }kathaya deveśa rahaḥ kāle maheśvara||</TEXT>
<TEXT> bhagavān{ }uvāca|*</TEXT>
<TEXT> pipāśāromaharṣaṃ ca vepanaṃ gātrasīdanam|</TEXT>
<TEXT> nidrāsvedaṃ ca tandrā ca muhūrtam{ }upajāyate||</TEXT>
<TEXT> nikledatvaṃ kharatvaṃ ca yonyāt{ }samupajāyate|</TEXT>
<TEXT> na cārdravaṃvai dṛśyeta śukrasya rajaso 'pi vā| </TEXT>
<TEXT> sadyogṛhītagarbhāyā liṅgāny{ }etāni tattvataḥ||</TEXT>
<TEXT> devy{ }uvāca|*</TEXT>
<TEXT> kena liṅgena vijñeyaṃ putrajanma maheśvara|</TEXT>
<TEXT> kanyakā kena liṅgena jñāyate kathayasva me||</TEXT>
<TEXT> bhagavān{ }uvāca|*</TEXT>
<TEXT> pādorujaṅghapārśvaś{ }ca dakṣiṇaṃ yadi hy{ }unnataḥ|</TEXT>
<TEXT> dakṣiṇaṃ vipulaṃ tatra tadā putraḥ prajāyate||</TEXT>
<TEXT> vāmaś{ }caiva yadā paśyet{ }tadā jāyeta kanyakā|</TEXT>
<TEXT> unnataṃ madhyamasthāś{ }ca tadā jāyet - napuṃsakam||</TEXT>
<TEXT> devy{ }uvāca|*</TEXT>
<TEXT> puṃsā kapolaromāni khalitaṃ kena jāyate|</TEXT>
<TEXT> kathaṃ strīṇāṃ na jāyeta romāṇi khalitaṃ tathā||</TEXT>
%Naraharinatha p.638
<TEXT> bhagavān{ }uvāca|*</TEXT>
<TEXT> tathā vṛṣaṇagā jantor yasya retovahā śiraḥ|</TEXT>
<TEXT> nibaddhā mastake tālu kapolās{ }tu samāśritāḥ||</TEXT>
<TEXT> taiḥ kapoleṣu romāṇi jāyante antaretasaḥ|</TEXT>
<TEXT> khalitaṃ śukradoṣeṇa narāṇām{ }upajāyate||</TEXT>
<TEXT> śirā śukravahā strīṇāṃ na śūnyasyānna jāyate|</TEXT>
<TEXT> yātmāpālo ca kās{ }tv{ }agni dṛṣṭimaṇḍalasaṃśritaḥ ?||</TEXT>
<TEXT> śoṇitai soktikoṣṭasthanniśoṣayati tattvataḥ|</TEXT>
<TEXT> nibaddhanty{ }akṣipakṣmāṇi tena romāṇi ca bhruvoḥ||</TEXT>
<TEXT> aśukratvāc{ }ca nārīṇāṃ khalitaṃ nopajāyate|</TEXT>
<TEXT> chāyāvyapagatasnehā rukṣāgātraśiroruhā|</TEXT>
<TEXT> grasatosmābhajaṭharā mṛtagarbhaḥ prajāyate||</TEXT>
<TEXT> devy{ }uvāca|*</TEXT>
<TEXT> somadhātu kathaṃ jñeyā agnidhātus{ }tatheśvara|</TEXT>
<TEXT> pṛthagbhāgaviśeṣeṇa kathayasva maheśvara||</TEXT>
<TEXT> bhagavān{ }uvāca|*</TEXT>
<TEXT> śleṣmamedas{ }tathā snāyuḥ asthidantanakhāni ca|</TEXT>
<TEXT> striyās{ }tanyaś{ }ca śukraś{ }ca yac{ }ca śvetaṃ tathākṣiṣu||</TEXT>
<TEXT> eteṣāṃ saumyabhāgatvāc{ }chvetatvam{ }upajāyate|</TEXT>
<TEXT> āgneyabhāvād{ }raktatvaṃ kṛṣṇatvaṃ cāpi gacchati||</TEXT>
<TEXT> tvagmāṃsarudhiraṃ majjādṛṣṭiroma tathaiva ca|</TEXT>
<TEXT> āgneyadhātusomaś{ }ca kathito 'smi varānane|</TEXT>
<TEXT> brūhi brūhi viśālākṣi yady{ }asti tava saṃśayaḥ||</TEXT>

<CHAPTER>15 jīvavarṇanam</CHAPTER>
%15.1:
<TEXT> devy{ }uvāca|*</TEXT>
<TEXT> jīvabhūteti yat{ }proktaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ kīdṛśaṃ bhavet|</TEXT>
        <APP>\va <LEM>lakṣaṇaṃ</LEM> \Ed; lakṣaṇāṅ \msCa</APP>
<TEXT> sthānam{ }asya na jānāmi rūpaṃ varṇaṃ ca īśvara||</TEXT>
        % sthāna is illegible in \msCa
        % rūpavarṇa \Ed
%15.2:
<TEXT> etat{ }kautūhalaṃ chindhi saṃśayaṃ parameśvara|</TEXT>
% phps anya-deva?
% stem form nirṇaya(ṃ)
<TEXT> na cānyad{ }eva paśyāmi jīvanirṇaya kīrtaya||</TEXT>
%15.3:
<TEXT> īśvara uvāca|*</TEXT>
        <APP>\vo <LEM>īśvara</LEM> \msCa; bhagavān \Ed</APP>
<TEXT> jīvasya lakṣaṇaṃ devi kathituṃ kena śakyate|</TEXT>
        <APP>\va <LEM>lakṣaṇaṃ</LEM> \Ed; kathitaṃ \msCa </APP>
% stem form rūpavarṇa or bha-vipulā rūpavarṇaṃ
<TEXT> na rūpavarṇa jīvasya vidyate sthānam{ }eva ca||</TEXT>

%            for masc gender (em. to vyāpi) 
%15.4:
<TEXT> vyāpī sarvagataṃ sūkṣmaṃ sarvam{ }āśritya tiṣṭhati|</TEXT>

<TEXT> prayāti lokaṃ jagadīśvarasya</TEXT>
<TEXT> vimānayānaiḥ sahito 'psarobhiḥ|</TEXT>
<TEXT> ekaikasiṣṭasya sahasravarṣam</TEXT>
<TEXT> annaprado modati devaloke||</TEXT>

<TEXT> cyutaś{ }ca martye sa bhaved{ }dhanāḍhyaḥ</TEXT>
<TEXT> kulodgataḥ sarvaguṇopapannaḥ|</TEXT>
<TEXT> yaśaḥ śriyaṃ sarvakalajñatā ca</TEXT>
<TEXT> bhavet{ }sa bhogī sakalatraputraḥ||</TEXT>

<TEXT> dadyād{ }daridraḥ kṛpaṇārtadīno</TEXT>
<TEXT> bālāgadatvāturamāgatānām|</TEXT>
<TEXT> tṛṣṇābubhukṣāgatikāgatānām</TEXT>
<TEXT> dattvā sadharmasya phalaṃ kaniṣṭa||</TEXT>

<TEXT> vāṇijyadharmādiphalāśritānām</TEXT>
<TEXT> dharmo hi tasya na ca nirmalo 'sti|</TEXT>
<TEXT> toyaṃ ca dadyāl{ }laghupūrṇakambham</TEXT>
<TEXT> śītaṃ sugandhaṃ parivāritaṃ ca||</TEXT>

<TEXT> sa yāti lokaṃ salileśvarasya</TEXT>
<TEXT> na tasya janmānitṛṣābhibhūtaḥ|</TEXT>
<TEXT> upānahaṃ yo dadati dvijāya</TEXT>
%hypermetrical
<TEXT> suśobhanaṃ tailasudī surapitaṃ ca||</TEXT>

<TEXT> te yānti lokam{ }amarādhipasya</TEXT>
<TEXT> yamālayaṃ kaṣṭapathāna yānti|</TEXT>
<TEXT> prakṣīṇapuṇyā punar{ }atra loke</TEXT>
<TEXT> jāto bhaved{ }divyakulopapannaḥ||</TEXT>

<TEXT> dhanaiḥ samṛddhodhopatitvatāś{ }ca</TEXT>
<TEXT> rathāś{ }ca nāgā prabhavanti tasya|</TEXT>
<TEXT> vastrapradānena bhavanti devi</TEXT>
<TEXT> rūpottamasarvakalajñatāṃ ca||</TEXT>

<TEXT> samṛddhisaubhāgyaguṇānvitāś{ }ca</TEXT>
<TEXT> svargacyutās{ }te puruṣā bhavanti|</TEXT>
<TEXT> vastrapradānābhiratasya puṃsaḥ</TEXT>
<TEXT> anyat{ }pravakṣyāmi tataḥ praśastām||</TEXT>

<TEXT> vastraṃ tu lokeṣv{ }atipūjanīyam</TEXT>
<TEXT> vastraṃ narāṇāṃ tv{ }atimānanīyam|</TEXT>
<TEXT> vastraṃ tu bhūyo na ca mānalābhaḥ</TEXT>
<TEXT> parābhavaś{ }cāti jugupsanaś{ }ca||</TEXT>

<TEXT> tasmād{ }dhi vastraṃ satataṃ pradeyam</TEXT>

<TEXT> yāvanti sūtrāṇi bhavanti vastre</TEXT>
<TEXT> tāvad{ }yugaṃ gacchanti somalokam||</TEXT>

<TEXT> puṇyakṣayāj{ }jāyati mṛtyuloke</TEXT>
<TEXT> vastraprabhūte dhanadhānyakīrṇo ?|</TEXT>
<TEXT> surūpasaubhāgyayaśaśivanaś{ }ca</TEXT>
<TEXT> vidyādharo lokaprabhutvatāś{ }ca||</TEXT>

% unmetr or cch as short
<TEXT> dvijebhyac{ }chatraṃ sukṛtaṃ pradadyāt</TEXT>
<TEXT> varṣātapatraṃ dṛḍhaśobhanaṃ ca|</TEXT>
<TEXT> aṅgāravarṣatraṣu khaḍgamādyam</TEXT>
<TEXT> asaṃśayaṃ trāyati yāmyamārge||</TEXT>

<TEXT> svargaṃ ca yānti grahanāyakaś{ }ca</TEXT>
<TEXT> sa varṣakoṭyāyutam{ }antakāle|</TEXT>
<TEXT> jāyanti te mānuṣamartyaloke</TEXT>
<TEXT> gṛhottame bhogapatir{ }bhavanti||</TEXT>

<TEXT> kṛtvā maṭhaṃ śobhanavipradātā</TEXT>
<TEXT> dravyeṇa śuddhena tu pūjayitvā|</TEXT>
<TEXT> sa yāti devendrasadaṃ yatheṣṭam</TEXT>
<TEXT> savarṣakoṭiśatadivyasaṃkhyaiḥ||</TEXT>

<TEXT> tadantakāle yadi mānuṣatvam</TEXT>
<TEXT> jāyanti te saptamahīprabhoktā|</TEXT>
<TEXT> sa saptarathyatrayasamprayuktā</TEXT>
<TEXT> balādhiko yajñasahasrakartā||</TEXT>

<TEXT> bhūmipradātā dvijahīnadīnam</TEXT>
<TEXT> saṃmṛddhasasyo jalasaṃnikṛṣta|</TEXT>

<TEXT> vimānayānena manohareṇa||</TEXT>

<TEXT> manvantaraṃ yāvad{ }abhuktabhogān</TEXT>
<TEXT> tadantakāle cyutamartyaloke|</TEXT>
<TEXT> sa javamukhaṇḍādhipatir{ }bhavet</TEXT>
<TEXT> vīryānvito rājasahasranāthaḥ||</TEXT>

<TEXT> sa cailaghaṇṭāṃ kanakāgraśṛṅgām</TEXT>
<TEXT> dogdhīṃ savatsāṃ payasāṃ dvijānām|</TEXT>
<TEXT> dattvā dvijebhyaḥ samalaṅkṛtānām</TEXT>
<TEXT> prayānti lokaṃ surabhīsutānām||</TEXT>

<TEXT> yāvanti romāṇi bhavanti gāvaḥ</TEXT>
        <APP>\va <LEM>yāvanti</LEM> \Ed; prayānti \msCa</APP>

<TEXT> tasmāc{ }cyutā martyamahībhujās{ }te</TEXT>

<TEXT> bhuktvā yatheṣṭaṃ kramadevalokān</TEXT>
<TEXT> cyutaṃ ca martye sa bhaven{ }narendraḥ|</TEXT>
<TEXT> sudurjayaḥ śakrasahasrajetā</TEXT>

<TEXT> ahiṃsako jāyati dīrgham{ }āyuḥ</TEXT>

<TEXT> kālatrayaṃ snānakṛtena rājyaṃ</TEXT>
<TEXT> pītvā ca vāyus{ }tridaśādhipatvam||</TEXT>

<TEXT> anaśnatāyāḥ phalam{ }īśaloke</TEXT>

%Naraharinatha p.648
% unmetr  hypermetrical

<TEXT> satyaṃ vaded{ }yo 'pi ca dharmaśīlo</TEXT>
<TEXT> modaty{ }asau devi sahāpsarobhiḥ||</TEXT>

<TEXT> rasās{ }tu ṣaḍyo parivarjayanti</TEXT>
% stem form saubhāgya !
<TEXT> atīva saubhāgya labheta sādhvī|</TEXT>
<TEXT> dānena bhogān{ }atulyaṃ labheta</TEXT>
% licence bra
<TEXT> cirāyutāṃ yāti hi brahmacaryāt||</TEXT>

<TEXT> dhanāḍhyatāṃ yānti hi puṇyakarmān</TEXT>

<TEXT> kāmakrodhobhakūlā karimakarajhaṣā grāhakāmā bhayante</TEXT>
<TEXT> mṛtyor{ }ākhyārṇave 'smin{ }na śaraṇavivaśākāladṛṣṭo prayāti||</TEXT>

<TEXT> nityaṃ yena vinā na yāti divasaṃ pañcatvam{ }āpadyate</TEXT>
% unmetr śrigāla?
<TEXT> tyaktvā deha vanāntareṣu viṣame śvānaśrigālākule|</TEXT>
% nirvatate was typo ?
<TEXT> bandhuḥ sarvanivartate gatadayā dharmaika tatra sthitaḥ</TEXT>
% unmetr , cānyasuhṛdaḥ?
<TEXT> tasmād{ }dharmaparo na cānyaḥ suhṛdaḥ sevet{ }paratrārthinaḥ||</TEXT>

        <PARAL>\vo Ł The next XX verses are parallel to a passage in the Bṛhatkālottara (NGMPP Reel No.\ B 29/59 Manuscript No.\ pra - 89): $
        prāṇopānaḥ samānaś{ }ca udāno vyāna eva ca||
        nāgaḥ kurmodhva kṛkaro devadattadhanaṃyayau|
        prāṇas{ }tu prathamo vāyur{ }daśānām{ }api sa prabhuḥ||
        prāṇaḥ prāṇamayaḥ prāṇa visargāpūraṇaṃ prati|
        nityam{ }āpūrayaty{ }eṣa prāṇinām{ }urasi sthitaḥ||
        niśvāsocchvāsakāmais{ }tu prāṇo jīvasamāśritaḥ|
        prayāṇaṃ kurute yasmāt{ }tasmāt{ }prāṇa prakīrtitaḥ||
        apānasahāpānas{ }tu āhāraṃ ca nṛṇām{ }adhaḥ|
        mūtraśukravahovāyur{ }apānas{ }tena kīrtitaḥ||
        pītaṃ bhakṣitam{ }āghrātaṃ raktapitakaphānilaṃ|
        samaṃ nayati mātreṣu samāno nāma mārutaḥ||
        spadaṃyabhyadharaṃ vaktraṃ netragātra prakopanaḥ|
        udvejayati marmāṇi udāto nāma mārutaḥ||
        vyāno vināmayatyaṃgaṃ vyāno vyādhiprakopakaḥ|
        prītecināsī kathito vāddhikyāt vyāna ucyate||;
        Ł cf.\ also Sārdhatriśatikālottara, Agnipurāṇa and Dīpikā by Aghoraśivācārya on the Mṛgendra $ </PARAL>

<TEXT> aho matimatāṃ śreṣṭha aho dharmabhṛtāṃ vara|</TEXT>
        <!-- <TR>Bravo, O best of the wise, bravo, O best of the ones who maintain Dharma! </TR> -->
        <APP>\va <LEM>matimatāṃ</LEM> \msCamsCbmsCc\msNa; matimanā \Ed</APP>
        <APP>\vb <LEM>vara</LEM> \msCa\msCc\msNa; varaḥ \msCb\Ed</APP>

%               śamaḥ metri causa!
<TEXT> aho dama śamaḥ satya aho yajña aho tapaḥ||</TEXT>
        <!-- <TR>Bravo self-control, bravo tranquillity! Bravo sacrifice, bravo penance!</TR> -->
        <APP>\vc <LEM>dama śamaḥ</LEM> \msCa\msCb\msNa; damaḥ śamaḥ \msCc\Ed</APP>
% \msNa\ 231.jpg lower image
<TEXT> anenāmṛtavākyena vismayo me paro gataḥ|</TEXT>
        <!-- <TR>By this nectar-like speech [of yours], my amazement has risen considerably.</TR> -->
<TEXT> prīto 'smi ca tapādhārajñānādbhutarasena ca||</TEXT>
        <!-- <TR>And I am pleased with the extraordinary flavour of knowledge based on penance.</TR> -->
        <APP>\vc <LEM>prīto 'smi ca</LEM> \msCb\msCc\msNa\Ed; \uncl{pr}×× ca \msCa</APP>
        <APP>\vd <LEM>°bhuta°</LEM> \msCamsCbmsCc\msNa; °bhūta° \Ed</APP>
% vara shd be masc.
<TEXT> kiṃ dadāmi varaṃ brūhi dātāsmi tava cepsitam|</TEXT>

        <APP>\vb <LEM>cepsitam</LEM> \msCa\msCc\msNa\Ed; cesmitam \msCb</APP>

<TEXT> athavā bhagavān{ }viṣṇur{ }mama jijñāsur{ }āgataḥ||</TEXT>
                <!-- <TR>Or rather [you must be] Lord Viṣṇu, who has come to test me.</TR> -->
<TEXT> vyaktaṃ tvāṃ puruṣaśreṣṭha jānāmi puruṣottama|</TEXT>
        <!-- <TR>I recognize you clearly, O best of men, O highest person!</TR> -->

                 <LEM>°śreṣṭha</LEM> \msCamsCbmsCc\msNa; °śreṣṭhaḥ \Ed</APP>
         <APP>\vb <LEM>puruṣottama</LEM> \msCb\msNa;
                 \uncl{pu}××ttama \msCa, puruṣotta× \msCc, puruṣottamaḥ \Ed</APP>
<TEXT> rūpaṃ darśaya govinda yady{ }asti tapasaḥ phalam||</TEXT>
        <!-- <TR>Display your [true] Form, O Govinda, if penance can yield fruit.</TR> -->
        <APP>\vc <LEM>rūpaṃ darśaya govinda</LEM> \msCa\msCb\msNa\Ed;

        <!-- <TR>My birth and my austerities have now borne their fruits.</TR> -->

                                        \uncl{sva}sūkṣma° \msNb, sasūkṣmaṃ \Ed</APP>

<SUBCHAPTER>paramāṇuḥ</SUBCHAPTER>
<TEXT> adhunānyat{ }pravakṣyāmi paramāṇu caturvidham|</TEXT>
        <!-- <TR>...................</TR> -->
% \msNa\ 234.jpg
<TEXT> pārthivādicaturbhūtair{ }yair{ }vyāptaṃ nikhilaṃ jagat||</TEXT>
<TEXT> lakṣaṇaṃ tasya rājendra śṛṇu vakṣyāmi sāmpratam|</TEXT>
<TEXT> pārthivordhagatiḥ ! sūkṣmaḥ paramāṇur{ }narādhipa||</TEXT>
<TEXT> pratyakṣadarśanaṃ dhyānaṃ lakṣayan{ }niyataḥ śuciḥ|</TEXT>
<TEXT> mucyate sarvapāpebhyo rāhunā candramā yathā||</TEXT>
<TEXT> tena yo 'bhyasate nityaṃ sa yogī bhuvaneśvara|</TEXT>
<TEXT> adhogati mahārāja paramāṇu jalodbhuvaḥ||</TEXT>
<TEXT> abhyased{ }yad{ }idaṃ rājan{ }sarvapātakanāśanam|</TEXT>
<TEXT> āgneyaparamāṇuś{ }ca tiryagūrdhagatiḥ ! smṛtāḥ||</TEXT>
<TEXT> ya idaṃ dhyāyate nityam{ }uttamāṃ gatim{ }āpnuyāt|</TEXT>
<TEXT> vāyavyaṃ paramāṇuś{ }ca adhordhvatiryag{ }āsmṛtā||</TEXT>
<TEXT> na sa muhyati taṃ dṛṣṭvā vāyusambhava bhūpate|</TEXT>
<TEXT> catvāra ete rājendra paramāṇur{ }nirīkṣate||</TEXT>
<TEXT> tena sarvamakhairiṣṭaṃ tena taptaṃ taptaṃ tathā|</TEXT>
<TEXT> tena dattā mahī kṛtsnā saptasāgarasaṃvṛtā||</TEXT>
% unmetr (two short), unless licence kri
<TEXT> sarvatīrthābhiṣekaś{ }ca sarvavratakriyā tathā|</TEXT>
<TEXT> anenaiva vidhānena daśadhyānaṃ narādhipa|</TEXT>
<TEXT> kurute avyavacchinnaṃ sarvakāmaphalapradam||</TEXT>



<SUBCHAPTER>daśākṣaramantraḥ</SUBCHAPTER>
<TEXT> daśākṣaramahārāja yogīndrasya mahātmanaḥ|</TEXT>
%Naraharinatha p.668
% \msCa\ 462.jpg line 4
% \msNa\ 234.jpg upper line 4
<TEXT> kathayāmi samāsena śṛṇuṣvāvahito bhava||</TEXT>
%      OṂ OṂ OṂ
<TEXT> praṇavādisvarā trīṇi dīrghabindusamāyutam|</TEXT>
%         Ñ? or JHA?          Y-
<TEXT> pañca pañca cavarge tu vāyubījam{ }adhasthitam||</TEXT>
% pañcamaṃ ca cavarge tu?
%  adhaḥsthitam \msCb; adha\uncl{ḥsthitam} \msCa, CHECK \msNa
% unmetr (two short)
%       -O
<TEXT> trayodaśasvarāyuktaṃ pañcama parikīrtitam|</TEXT>
%              ×yodaśa \msCa            pañcame \msCa\msCb\msNa
%      JHA               
<TEXT> pañcaviṃśatimaḥ ṣaṣṭha akṣaraḥ parikīrtitaḥ||</TEXT>
%                      ṣaṣṭhaḥ \msCa\msCb\msNa
%       Y-
<TEXT> yādṛśaṃ pañcamaḥ proktaṃ saptame ca prayojayet|</TEXT>
%  pañcameḥ \msCa              pañcame \msCb\msNa
%      -Ā
<TEXT> akārasvarasaṃyuktaṃ sarvapātakanāśanam||</TEXT>
%      ākāra \msCa\msNa
%                               PI
<TEXT> prathamaṃ pañcame varge tṛtīyasvarayojitam|</TEXT>
%     KṢĪ?? or HĀ (ākāra) or HĪ 
<TEXT> uktare kārasaṃyuktaṃ navamaṃ parikīrtitam||</TEXT>
% uttare \msCa\msCa\msNa         kā××××××××rikīrtitam \msCa
%      OṂ
% OṂ OṂ OṂ JHA YO   JHA YĀ PI KṢĪ OṂ
<TEXT> daśamaḥ punar{ }oṃkāraḥ mantraśreṣṭho daśākṣaraḥ|</TEXT>
% CHECK \msCa, oṅkārau \msCb, CHECK \msNa
<TEXT> japato dhyāyate vāpi pārthivādi krameṇa tu||</TEXT>
<TEXT> mucyate so 'pi saṃsāre saṃśayo nāsti bhūpate|</TEXT>
<TEXT> ācāramūlo dharmas{ }tu dharmamūlo janārdanaḥ|</TEXT>
<TEXT> tena sarvajagad{ }vyāptaṃ trailokyaṃ sa carācaraṃ||</TEXT>

%      - - -     . .  -  .  -  . .  . -     -  -     .  -  - . -
<TEXT> ācārāt{ }katidhāṅga kīrtaya punas{ }tṛptir{ }na me jāyate|</TEXT>
<TEXT> sarvajñaḥ tvam{ }ahaṃ śṛṇomi varadaṃ kiñcin{ }na me śāśvaram</TEXT>
%       -     -  -  . .   -  . - . .  . -?- - . - -  . -
<TEXT> tan{ }me kīrtaya dharmasāraśubhadam{ }ācāramūlāśrayam||</TEXT>

<TEXT> vaiśampāyana uvāca|*</TEXT>

<TEXT> nityaṃ namraśirodvijātiguruṣu śuśrūṣaṇaṃ daivatam</TEXT>
<TEXT> tiṣṭhenācamanena cāśanakaraṃ vāmāsthimānādaram|</TEXT>
% unmetr
<TEXT> sūryāgniśaśibandhur{ }āryapurataḥ kuryān{ }na cāvaśyakam</TEXT>
<TEXT> śasye bhasmani govrajedvijajalaṃ kuryān{ }na cārkaṃ naraḥ||</TEXT>

<TEXT> pādenāgnijalaṃ spṛśen{ }na ca guruṃ pādena pādaṃ tathā</TEXT>
<TEXT> śaucaṃ kārya jalādinā ca niyataṃ nādho jalaṃ kārayet|</TEXT>
<TEXT> kuryān{ }nityabhivādanaṃ dvijaguror{ }mātāpitṛr{ }daivatam</TEXT>
<TEXT> etācāravidhiḥ samāsaniyamas{ }tubhyaṃ mayā kīrtitam||</TEXT>
%Naraharinatha p.669
<ANUSTUBH/>
<TEXT> janamejaya uvāca|*</TEXT>
% metre=śārdūlavikrīḍita <NOTANUSTUBH/>
%       -  -   -  . . -  . - . . . -? -  - . -   -  . -
<TEXT> strīṇāṃ kiṃ priyam{ }asti tad{ }vada vibho saṃsārasārastriyām</TEXT>
<TEXT> kiṃ sadbhāva na vedmi tasya viṣaye kiṃ dveṣya kiṃ tātpriyam|</TEXT>
%      -   - -?
<TEXT> paśyāmi na ca tasya garbhakalayā prāpnoti niḥsaṃśayam</TEXT>
<TEXT> māyājālasahasragāpi yuvatī kurvanti bhartā priyam||</TEXT>

<TEXT> vaiśampāyana uvāca|*</TEXT>
% metre=śārdūlavikrīḍita <NOTANUSTUBH/>
%       -  -    -    . .    -  . -   . . . -   -  - .  -  -    .  -
<TEXT> rājan{ }kiṃ priyam{ }asti arthaparataḥ paśyāmi nānyan{ }nṛpe</TEXT>
%       -  -   -  .  . - .  -  . . . -    - -  .  -  - .  -
%      licence    .pr !
<TEXT> putrārthaikaprayojanaṃ yuvatayaḥ svāyambhuvoktāmaraiḥ|</TEXT>
% unmetr
<TEXT> kāntā nityakalā pravartanakarī dharmasakhāyā satī</TEXT>
<TEXT> māyā vāpi karoti sadya manujātyaktānya vā sevate||</TEXT>

<TEXT> strīsaṅgaṃ parivarjayen{ }narapate āyāsadaṃ duḥkhadam</TEXT>
%                                    !
% unmetr
<TEXT> mṛtyudvārabhayākaraṃ viṣagṛham{ }āpat{ }sughorālayam|</TEXT>
%                                  !
<TEXT> agnir{ }mārutamattavāraṇasama tasyānugāmī sadā</TEXT>
%                                     !
<TEXT> strīhetor{ }hatarāvaṇastridaśapa indro 'pi visthāpitaḥ|</TEXT>
<TEXT> strīhetor{ }api candramāstribhuvane dhiktāṃ gataś{ }cāmaro|</TEXT>
<TEXT> daṇḍakṣo hatarāṣṭrapaurasahitaḥ kiṃ bhūya vakṣyāmy{ }aham||</TEXT>
<TEXT> janamejaya uvāca|*</TEXT>
<ANUSTUBH/>
% metre=śārdūlavikrīḍita <NOTANUSTUBH/>
%       -  -  - . . -  . -    . . .  -   - -     . -     -  . -
<TEXT> vipro kīdṛśalakṣaṇaṃ bhavati bho kīdṛg{ }muniś{ }cocyate</TEXT>
<TEXT> kenārthena bhaveta bhikṣu bhagavan{ }nighnanti ko vā dvija|</TEXT>
<TEXT> kenārthena bhaved{ }dvijendra bhagavān{ }jñeyaḥ parivrājakaḥ</TEXT>
% unmetrical
<TEXT> ! jñeyāḥ kim{ }ṛṣayaś{ }ca lakṣaṇamuner{ }icchāmi jñātuṃ punaḥ||</TEXT>
<ANUSTUBH/>
<TEXT> vaiśampāyana uvāca|*</TEXT>
% metre=śārdūlavikrīḍita <NOTANUSTUBH/>
%       -  -    -    . .    -  . -   . . . -   -  - .  -  -    .  -
<TEXT> satyaṃ śaucam{ }ahiṃsatā damaśamau bhūtānukampī sadā</TEXT>
<TEXT> ātmā rāmajito svadharmanirataḥ sattvastha nityaṃ manaḥ|</TEXT>
<TEXT> kāmakrodhayamasvadāranirataḥ saṃtyajya lobhaḥ śanaiḥ</TEXT>
<TEXT> evaṃ yaḥ kurute dvijātisuvaraḥ śūdro 'pi yaḥ saṃyamī||</TEXT>

<TEXT> tasmāc{ }chadmakavarjitaḥ sa bhagavān{ }saṃsārabhībhidyakaḥ</TEXT>
<TEXT> yat{ }tat{ }sthānaparaṃ vrajanti puruṣāḥ tasmāt{ }parivrājakaḥ|</TEXT>
%            !
<TEXT> granthi dārasutaṃ dhanaṃś{ }ca virati nirgranthika socyate</TEXT>
<TEXT> ramyante ṛṣirāśrame dhṛtimanas{ }tasmād{ }ṛṣiḥ socyate||</TEXT>
%Naraharinatha p.670
<TEXT> kāyavāṅmanadaṇḍatatparataras{ }te daṇḍikarūcyate</TEXT>
% licence only second śra!!!
<TEXT> saddharmaśravaṇaṃ vadanti śravaṇaḥ saddharmabrahmākṣaraḥ|</TEXT>
<TEXT> pāśaprakṣipataṃ paśutvasakalaṃ pāśūpatās{ }te smṛtāḥ</TEXT>
% Pāśupatas!
<TEXT> vipre pāśupatādibhikṣusakalaṃ pṛṣṭo 'smy{ }ahaṃ lakṣaṇam||</TEXT>

<TEXT> sarvaṃ tat{ }kathito 'si lakṣaṇa mayā sandhiśvanirnāśanam</TEXT>
<TEXT> prajñāsaṃgrahaśītavardhanaparaṃ saṃsāranirmūlanam|</TEXT>

<CHAPTER>23 nidrotpattiḥ</CHAPTER>

        <APP>\va <LEM>°tpattiṃ vikāraṃ ca</LEM> \msNa;
                      °tpattiṃ vikāraś{ }ca \Ed, 
                      °tpa\uncl{tti}×××× \msCa</APP>
<TEXT> tasmān{ }nidrāṃ na seveta tamomohapravardhanīm||</TEXT>
        <APP>\vd <LEM>°vardhanīm</LEM> \msCa; °vardhanī \msNa\Ed</APP>

<TEXT> <COLOPHON>iti vṛṣasārasaṃgrahe nidrotpattis{ }trayoviṃśatimo 'dhyāyaḥ</COLOPHON></TEXT>
        <APP> ŁColophon: $  <LEM>°viṃśatimo</LEM> \msCa\msNa; °viṃśatitamo \Ed</APP>

<TEXT> niṣadho nīlamadhye tu meruḥ śailamanoramaḥ||</TEXT>
<TEXT> praviṣṭaṣoḍaśādhas{ }tāṃ caturāśītim{ }ucchṛtaḥ|</TEXT>

<TEXT> yojanānāṃ sahasrāṇi dvātriṃśad{ }ūrdha ! vistṛtaḥ||</TEXT>

<TEXT> devarājo 'marāvatyām{ }agnis{ }tejovatī pure||</TEXT>

<TEXT> naiṛtir{ }vasati nityaṃ ramye śuddhavatī pure||</TEXT>

<TEXT> uttare paścime caiva pūrvadakṣiṇatas{ }tathā|</TEXT>

<TEXT> bhadrāśvaṃ plāvayitvā tu vanāny{ }upavanāni ca|</TEXT>

        <APP>\va <LEM>°vāra°</LEM> \msCa; °cāra° \Ed</APP>
<TEXT> yathāntavartī bahivartin{ }eva|</TEXT>
        <APP>\vb <LEM>yathāntava°</LEM> \Ed; yathāntarvva \msCa</APP>
<APP>
                 <LEM>°vartin{ }eva</LEM> \Ed; vartti\uncl{ne}va \msCa</APP>
% stem form
<TEXT> bhuñjanti bhogān{ }satatāntavartī</TEXT>
        <APP>\vc <LEM>bhuñjanti bhogān</LEM> \Ed; \uncl{bhuñja} ××× \msCa</APP>
<TEXT> kleśādhikaṃ nitya bahiḥsthitānām||</TEXT>

% unmetrical?
<TEXT> yathaiva rājā kariṇo ntardantam</TEXT>
        <APP>\va <LEM>kariṇo ntardantam</LEM> \msCa; kariṇāntadantadattam \Ed</APP>
<TEXT> bhuñjanti bhogān{ }satataṃ narendra|</TEXT>
        <APP>\vb <LEM>bhuñjanti</LEM> \Ed; bhujanti \msCa</APP>
%Naraharinatha p.678
% unmetrical?
<TEXT> yudhyeta rājā bahirdantabhogair</TEXT>
        <APP>\vc <LEM>bahirdantabhogair</LEM> \msCa; bahidattabhogair \Ed</APP>
<TEXT> yadantare paśya samānajātam||</TEXT>
        <APP>\vd <LEM>yadantare paśya samānajātam</LEM> \Ed; yadanta\uncl{re} ××××najātam \msCa</APP>

<TEXT> na dānatulyaṃ tv{ }abhayapradasya</TEXT>
<TEXT> na yajñatulyaṃ jita-indriyasya|</TEXT>
<TEXT> na cārthatulyaṃ jitakāminaś{ }ca</TEXT>
        <APP>\vc <LEM>°kāminaś{ }ca</LEM> \Ed; kāmina×× \msCa</APP>
<TEXT> na dharmatulyaṃ damakāmitasya||</TEXT>
        <APP>\vd <LEM>na dharmatulyaṃ</LEM> \Ed; ××××× \msCa</APP>
<APP>
                 <LEM>kāmitasya</LEM> \msCa; kāminasya \Ed</APP> 

<TEXT> bahvantaraṃ naiva hi dharmayoś{ }ca</TEXT>
<TEXT> kleśādhikaṃ bāhyaphalālpasāram|</TEXT>
<TEXT> yad{ }atra dharmaṃ phalanaiṣṭhikasya</TEXT>
<TEXT> na tulyakoṭī śatayājināpi||</TEXT>

<TEXT> etat{ }pavitraṃ paramaṃ sadharmam</TEXT>
<TEXT> purā yathoktaṃ parameśvareṇa|</TEXT>
<TEXT> mayāpi tulyaṃ kathitaṃ yathāvat</TEXT>
<TEXT> purāṇavedopaniṣatsusāram||</TEXT>

<TEXT> sadojasaubhāgyam{ }atīva medhā</TEXT>
<TEXT> nirutsukaḥ saumyam{ }anuttamaṃ ca|</TEXT>
<TEXT> suputrapautraṃ na vichinnagotram</TEXT>
% \msNc\ 257.jpg
<TEXT> bhavanti vidyādharalokapūjyam||</TEXT>

<TEXT> yaśaśriyaṃ kīrtir{ }atīva tejo</TEXT>
<TEXT> janapriyo dhānyadhanāyuvṛddhiḥ|</TEXT>
% licence pra
<TEXT> prabodhaprajñārujadharmavṛddhim</TEXT>
<TEXT> bhavanti te śāstrasadābhiyogī||</TEXT>

<TEXT> yaśasvinī āryasuvarṇaśṛṅgī</TEXT>
<TEXT> vedāntavipradvijagāyaneṣu|</TEXT>
<TEXT> dattvā phalaṃ tīrtham{ }anuttameṣu</TEXT>
<TEXT> śṛṇvanti ye tasya bhavet{ }sapuṇyam||</TEXT>

<TEXT> daśādhikaṃ vā ca catuś{ }ca puṇyam</TEXT>
<TEXT> śatādhikaṃ yaḥ paṭhitaprabhāte|</TEXT>
<TEXT> sahasraśaḥ pustakṛtasya puṇyam</TEXT>
%      -  -     .? -  -  . .  -  . - .  
<TEXT> paro 'bhyaste kīrtaya te yutāni||</TEXT>

<TEXT> adhītya yasyoragataṃ suśāstram</TEXT>
<TEXT> samastamadhyāyam{ }anukramena|</TEXT>
<TEXT> daśāyutāṅgo dadatuś{ }ca puṇyam</TEXT>
<TEXT> labhaty{ }asaṃdigdhayathādinaikaṃ||</TEXT>

% metre=sragdharā

% unmetr

<TEXT> yenedaṃ śāstrasāram{ }avikalamanasā yo 'bhyaseta prayatnāt</TEXT>
        <APP>\va <LEM>bhyaseta pra°</LEM> \Ed; bhyaset{ }tatpra° \msCa</APP>
<TEXT> vyakto 'sau siddhayogī bhavati ca niyataṃ yas{ }tu cittaprasannaḥ|</TEXT>
        <APP>\vb <LEM>sau</LEM> \Ed; so \msCa</APP>
<TEXT> pitryaṃ yo gītapūrvaṃ pratidinaśataśo urddhi yante ca sarve</TEXT>
        <APP>\vc <LEM>pitryaṃ yo gītapūrvaṃ</LEM> \msCa; nitya yo dhītayota pūrvvaṃ \Ed</APP>

                 <LEM>°dinaśataśo urddhi yante ca sarve</LEM> \Ed; \uncl{dina}×××××××××× \msCa</APP>
